    /*
     * Cookie Disclaimer to be included inline on the page
     * BMWDGTLTP-17749
     * author: ronny, skarzel
     */
    $(document).ready(function() {
      var CookieDisclaimer = function($component) {
        function buttonsInteractionSet() {
          $('.ds2-cookie-disclaimer-js--deny', $component).on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            triggerEvent('ds2-setRegulationRejected');
          });

          $('.ds2-cookie-disclaimer-js--submit', $component).on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            triggerEvent('ds2-setRegulationAccepted');
          });

          $('.ds2-cookie-disclaimer-js--close', $component).on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            triggerEvent('ds2-optoutConfirmed');
            triggerEvent('ds2-closeAll');
          });

          $('.ds2-cookie-disclaimer-js--button-close', $component).on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            triggerEvent('ds2-closeAll');
          });
        }

        function triggerEvent(pEvent) {
          var $window = window.digitals2.main.$window ? window.digitals2.main.$window : $(window);
          $window.trigger(pEvent);
        }

        buttonsInteractionSet();
      };

      function init() {
        var componentPath = "ds2-cookie-disclaimer";
        var $component = $('[data-component-path="' + componentPath + '"]');

        new CookieDisclaimer($component);
      }

      init();
    });
   </script>

   (function () {
  function pageBottom() {
    if (window['_satellite']) {
      _satellite.track('pageload_datalayer_ready');
    }
  }
  $(function() {
    var tracking = window.digitals2.tracking;
    tracking.api = tracking.impl.getInstance(window.digitalData || {pages: []});
    $(window).trigger('initializeTrackingComponents');
    if (window['cookiecontroller'] && window['cookiecontroller']['api']) {
      var ccApi = window.cookiecontroller.api;
      if (!ccApi.isInitialized()) {
        ccApi.registerOnInitialized(function () {
          pageBottom();
        });
      } else {
        pageBottom();
      }
    }
  });

  if (window['_satellite']) {
    _satellite.pageBottom();
  }
}());
